    41	/**
    42	 * Generate Product JSON-LD structured data
    43	 * Creates rich snippet for product pages with offers, images, and ratings
    44	 */
    45	export function generateProductSchema(
    46	  product: SchemaProduct,
    47	  selectedVariant?: SchemaVariant
    48	): object {
    49	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
    50	
    51	  // Get images from product media or variant media
    52	  const images: string[] = [];
    53	
    54	  if (selectedVariant?.media && selectedVariant.media.length > 0) {
    55	    // Use selected variant's media
    56	    const variantImages = selectedVariant.media
    57	      .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
    58	      .map((m) => m.url);
    59	    images.push(...variantImages);
    60	  } else if (product.media && product.media.length > 0) {
    61	    // Use product-level media
    62	    const productImages = product.media
    63	      .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
    64	      .map((m) => m.url);
    65	    images.push(...productImages);
    66	  } else if (product.images && product.images.length > 0) {
    67	    // Use legacy images field
    68	    images.push(...product.images);
    69	  } else if (product.variants && product.variants.length > 0) {
    70	    // Fallback: collect images from all variants if product has no direct media
    71	    for (const variant of product.variants) {
    72	      if (variant.media && variant.media.length > 0) {
    73	        const variantImages = variant.media
    74	          .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
    75	          .map((m) => m.url);
    76	        images.push(...variantImages);
    77	      }
    78	    }
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  // Calculate final price (with variant adjustment if applicable)
    82	  let finalPrice = product.price;
    83	  if (selectedVariant) {
    84	    finalPrice += selectedVariant.priceAdjust;
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  // Apply discount if exists
    88	  if (product.discount && product.discount > 0) {
    89	    finalPrice = finalPrice * (1 - product.discount / 100);
    90	  }
    91	
    92	  // Determine stock availability
    93	  let stock = product.stock;
    94	  if (selectedVariant) {
    95	    stock = selectedVariant.stock;
    96	  }
    97	
    98	  const availability =
    99	    stock > 0 ? 'https://schema.org/InStock' : 'https://schema.org/OutOfStock';
   100	
   101	  // Schema.org requires at least one image - use logo as absolute last resort
   102	  const schemaImages = images.length > 0 ? images : [`${baseUrl}/logo.png`];
   103	
   104	  const schema = {
   105	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   106	    '@type': 'Product',
   107	    name: selectedVariant
   108	      ? `${product.name} - ${selectedVariant.name}`
   109	      : product.name,
   110	    description: product.description || `${product.name} - ${siteConfig.name}`,
   111	    image: schemaImages,
   112	    ...(product.sku && { sku: product.sku }),
   113	    brand: {
   114	      '@type': 'Brand',
   115	      name: siteConfig.name,
   116	    },
   117	    offers: {
   118	      '@type': 'Offer',
   119	      price: finalPrice.toString(),
   120	      priceCurrency: siteLocale.currency,
   121	      availability,
   122	      url: `${baseUrl}/products/${product.slug || product.id}`,
   123	      ...(product.discount &&
   124	        product.discount > 0 && {
   125	          priceValidUntil: new Date(
   126	            Date.now() + 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000
   127	          ).toISOString(), // 30 days
   128	        }),
   129	    },
   130	  };
   131	
   132	  return schema;
   133	}
   134	
   135	/**
   136	 * Generate Organization JSON-LD structured data
   137	 * Should be included in the root layout for site-wide branding
   138	 */
   139	export function generateOrganizationSchema(): object {
   140	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   141	
   142	  return {
   143	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   144	    '@type': 'Organization',
   145	    name: siteConfig.name,
   146	    url: baseUrl,
   147	    logo: `${baseUrl}/logo.png`,
   148	    description: siteConfig.description,
   149	    contactPoint: {
   150	      '@type': 'ContactPoint',
   151	      contactType: 'customer support',
   152	      availableLanguage: siteLocale.language,
   153	    },
   154	  };
   155	}
   156	
   157	/**
   158	 * Generate BreadcrumbList JSON-LD structured data
   159	 * Shows navigation hierarchy (Home > Category > Subcategory > Product)
   160	 */
   161	export function generateBreadcrumbSchema(items: BreadcrumbItem[]): object {
   162	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   163	
   164	  const listItems = items.map((item, index) => ({
   165	    '@type': 'ListItem',
   166	    position: index + 1,
   167	    name: item.name,
   168	    item: item.url.startsWith('http') ? item.url : `${baseUrl}${item.url}`,
   169	  }));
   170	
   171	  return {
   172	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   173	    '@type': 'BreadcrumbList',
   174	    itemListElement: listItems,
   175	  };
   176	}
   177	
   178	/**
   179	 * Generate breadcrumb items for a product page
   180	 * Includes category hierarchy if available
   181	 */
   182	export function generateProductBreadcrumbs(
   183	  product: SchemaProduct,
   184	  categoryHierarchy?: Array<{ name: string; slug: string }>
   185	): BreadcrumbItem[] {
   186	  const items: BreadcrumbItem[] = [
   187	    {
   188	      name: 'Home',
   189	      url: '/',
   190	    },
   191	  ];
   192	
   193	  // Add category hierarchy if provided
   194	  if (categoryHierarchy && categoryHierarchy.length > 0) {
   195	    categoryHierarchy.forEach((category) => {
   196	      items.push({
   197	        name: category.name,
   198	        url: `/products?category=${category.slug}`,
   199	      });
   200	    });
   201	  } else if (product.category) {
   202	    // Fallback to just the direct category
   203	    items.push({
   204	      name: product.category.name,
   205	      url: `/products?category=${product.category.slug}`,
   206	    });
   207	  }
   208	
   209	  // Add the product itself
   210	  items.push({
   211	    name: product.name,
   212	    url: `/products/${product.slug || product.id}`,
   213	  });
   214	
   215	  return items;
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Generate WebSite JSON-LD structured data
   220	 * Includes site search capability
   221	 */
   222	export function generateWebSiteSchema(): object {
   223	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   224	
   225	  return {
   226	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   227	    '@type': 'WebSite',
   228	    name: siteConfig.name,
   229	    url: baseUrl,
   230	    potentialAction: {
   231	      '@type': 'SearchAction',
   232	      target: {
   233	        '@type': 'EntryPoint',
   234	        urlTemplate: `${baseUrl}/products?search={search_term_string}`,
   235	      },
   236	      'query-input': 'required name=search_term_string',
   237	    },
   238	  };
   239	}
   240	
   241	/**
   242	 * Helper function to inject JSON-LD script into the page
   243	 * Returns a script tag with type="application/ld+json"
   244	 */
   245	export function renderJsonLd(data: object): string {
   246	  return JSON.stringify(data);
   247	}

    10	async function postHandler(req: NextRequest) {
    11	  // Extract client info for activity logging
    12	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    13	
    14	  try {
    15	    const body = await req.json();
    16	    const { identifier, email, phone, password, name } = body;
    17	    const providedIdentifier = identifier || email || phone;
    18	
    19	    // Validate required fields (name is optional)
    20	    if (!providedIdentifier || !password) {
    21	      return NextResponse.json(
    22	        { error: 'ایمیل یا شماره تلفن به همراه رمز عبور الزامی هستند' },
    23	        { status: 400 }
    24	      );

    33	        { status: 400 }
    34	      );
    35	    }

    38	    // If name is not provided, use empty string as default

    40	      email: identifierType === 'email' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    41	      phone: identifierType === 'phone' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    42	      password,
    43	      name: name || '',
    44	    });

    55	      },

    58	        userId: user.id,
    59	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    60	      });
    61	    });
    62	
    63	    return NextResponse.json(
    64	      {

    66	        message: 'ثبت‌نام با موفقیت انجام شد',

    68	          id: user.id,

     9	/**
    10	 * Login endpoint - handles user authentication
    11	 * This endpoint is rate-limited by middleware (5 requests per 2 minutes)
    12	 * Returns user data which the client uses to trigger NextAuth session creation
    13	 */
    14	export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
    15	  // Extract client info for activity logging
    16	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    17	
    18	  try {
    19	    const body = await req.json();
    20	    const { email, password } = body;
    21	
    22	    // Validate input
    23	    if (!email || !password) {
    24	      return NextResponse.json(
    25	        { error: 'ایمیل و رمز عبور الزامی است' },
    26	        { status: 400 }
    27	      );
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    // Authenticate user (throws error if invalid)
    31	    const user = await authenticateUser(email, password);
    32	
    33	    log.info('User authenticated successfully', {
    34	      userId: user.id,
    35	      email: user.email,
    36	    });
    37	
    38	    // Log successful login (fire-and-forget)
    39	    logUserActivity({
    40	      userId: user.id,
    41	      activityType: 'LOGIN_SUCCESS',
    42	      ipAddress,
    43	      userAgent,
    44	      success: true,
    45	      metadata: {
    46	        identifier_type: email.includes('@') ? 'email' : 'phone',
    47	      },
    48	    }).catch((err) => {
    49	      log.warn('Failed to log login success', {
    50	        userId: user.id,
    51	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    52	      });
    53	    });
    54	
    55	    // Return user data and credentials for NextAuth signIn
    56	    return NextResponse.json({
    57	      success: true,
    58	      user: {
    59	        id: user.id,
    60	        email: user.email,
    61	        name: user.name,
    62	        role: user.role,
    63	      },
    64	    });
    65	  } catch (error) {
    66	    // Log failed login (fire-and-forget)
    67	    logUserActivity({
    68	      activityType: 'LOGIN_FAILED',
    69	      ipAddress,
    70	      userAgent,
    71	      success: false,
    72	      errorMessage: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Login failed',
    73	    }).catch((err) => {
    74	      log.warn('Failed to log login failure', {
    75	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    55	  return {
    56	    ...data,
    57	    createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
    58	    updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
    59	  };
    60	}

    62	/**
    63	 * Check if a user exists with the given identifier
    64	 * Used for uniqueness validation
    65	 */
    66	export async function checkUserExists(
    67	  identifier: { email?: string; phone?: string },
    68	  excludeUserId?: string
    69	): Promise<boolean> {
    70	  const supabase = createClient();
    71	
    72	  // Build OR conditions
    73	  const conditions = [];
    74	
    75	  if (identifier.email) {
    76	    conditions.push(`email.eq.${identifier.email}`);
    77	  }
    78	
    79	  if (identifier.phone) {
    80	    conditions.push(`phone.eq.${identifier.phone}`);
    81	  }
    82	
    83	  if (conditions.length === 0) {
    84	    return false;
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  let query = supabase
    88	    .from('users')
    89	    .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
    90	    .or(conditions.join(','));
    91	
    92	  if (excludeUserId) {
    93	    query = query.neq('id', excludeUserId);
    94	  }

/**
 * Persian text utility functions
 * Handles conversion between Persian and English characters
 */

/**
 * Map of Persian digits to English digits
 */
const persianDigits = ['۰', '۱', '۲', '۳', '۴', '۵', '۶', '۷', '۸', '۹'];
const arabicDigits = ['٠', '١', '٢', '٣', '٤', '٥', '٦', '٧', '٨', '٩'];

/**
 * Convert Persian/Arabic digits to English digits
 * @param text - Text containing Persian or Arabic digits
 * @returns Text with English digits
 */
export function convertPersianToEnglish(text: string): string {
  if (!text) return text;

  let result = text;

  // Convert Persian digits
  persianDigits.forEach((persianDigit, index) => {
    result = result.replace(new RegExp(persianDigit, 'g'), index.toString());
  });

  // Convert Arabic digits
  arabicDigits.forEach((arabicDigit, index) => {
    result = result.replace(new RegExp(arabicDigit, 'g'), index.toString());
  });

  return result;
}

/**
 * Check if text contains Persian/Arabic characters
 * @param text - Text to check
 * @returns true if text contains Persian/Arabic characters
 */
export function containsPersianCharacters(text: string): boolean {
  if (!text) return false;

  // Persian/Arabic Unicode ranges
  const persianPattern =
    /[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF]/;
  return persianPattern.test(text);
}

/**
 * Validate Persian name (allows Persian letters, spaces, and common Persian characters)
 * @param name - Name to validate
 * @returns true if name is valid Persian name
 */
export function isValidPersianName(name: string): boolean {
  if (!name || !name.trim()) return false;

  // Allow Persian letters, spaces, Arabic diacritics, and common Persian punctuation
  const persianNamePattern =
    /^[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF\s]+$/;
  return persianNamePattern.test(name.trim());
}

/**
 * Validate if text can be a valid name (Persian or English)
 * @param name - Name to validate
 * @returns true if name is valid (Persian or English letters)
 */
export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
  if (!name || !name.trim()) return false;

  // Allow Persian, Arabic, English letters, spaces, hyphens, and apostrophes
  const namePattern =
    /^[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFFa-zA-Z\s'-]+$/;
  return namePattern.test(name.trim());
}

/**
 * Normalize phone number by converting Persian/Arabic digits to English
 * @param phone - Phone number with potentially Persian/Arabic digits
 * @returns Normalized phone number with English digits
 */
export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
  if (!phone) return phone;

  // Convert Persian/Arabic digits to English
  const normalized = convertPersianToEnglish(phone);

  // Remove any non-digit characters except leading +
  return normalized.replace(/[^\d+]/g, '').replace(/\+(?=.)/g, '');
}

/**
 * Validate Iranian phone number format (09xxxxxxxxx)
 * Accepts both Persian and English digits
 * @param phone - Phone number to validate
 * @returns true if valid Iranian phone format
 */
export function isValidIranianPhone(phone: string): boolean {
  if (!phone) return false;

  // Normalize first
  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);

  // Check if matches Iranian phone format (09xxxxxxxxx - 11 digits starting with 09)
  return /^09\d{9}$/.test(normalized);
}

  // Allow Persian letters, spaces, Arabic diacritics, and common Persian punctuation
  const persianNamePattern =
    /^[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF\s]+$/;
  return persianNamePattern.test(name.trim());
}

/**
 * Validate if text can be a valid name (Persian or English)
 * @param name - Name to validate
 * @returns true if name is valid (Persian or English letters)
 */
export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
  if (!name || !name.trim()) return false;

  // Allow Persian, Arabic, English letters, spaces, hyphens, and apostrophes
  const namePattern =
    /^[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFFa-zA-Z\s'-]+$/;
  return namePattern.test(name.trim());
}

/**
 * Normalize phone number by converting Persian/Arabic digits to English
 * @param phone - Phone number with potentially Persian/Arabic digits
 * @returns Normalized phone number with English digits
 */
export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
  if (!phone) return phone;

  // Convert Persian/Arabic digits to English
  const normalized = convertPersianToEnglish(phone);

  // Remove any non-digit characters except leading +
  return normalized.replace(/[^\d+]/g, '').replace(/\+(?=.)/g, '');
}

/**
 * Validate Iranian phone number format (09xxxxxxxxx)
 * Accepts both Persian and English digits
 * @param phone - Phone number to validate
 * @returns true if valid Iranian phone format
 */
export function isValidIranianPhone(phone: string): boolean {
  if (!phone) return false;

  // Normalize first
  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);

  // Check if matches Iranian phone format (09xxxxxxxxx - 11 digits starting with 09)
  return /^09\d{9}$/.test(normalized);
}

codex
The patch introduces the locale/currency defaults but leaves key currency/date consumers and E2E assertions on the old Persian/Toman/Jalali assumptions. Those inconsistencies would surface in the UI and test suite.

Full review comments:

- [P2] Migrate cart formatter before changing shared currency — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/utils/format.ts:3-7
  With the shared formatter now defaulting to `siteLocale.currency` (USD by default), cart UI still imports `formatPrice` from `src/store/cart-store.ts`, whose local formatter remains hard-coded to `fa-IR` plus `تومان`. Product/search/wishlist surfaces that use this helper will show USD while cart drawer/summary shows Toman for the same prices, so users see inconsistent currencies until the store formatter is removed or wired to the same config.

- [P2] Replace remaining Jalali date call sites — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/utils/format.ts:14-23
  This adds config-driven date helpers, but existing date surfaces still bypass them: admin/profile pages and email/transaction components continue importing `date-fns-jalali` or formatting with `fa-IR`. Under the new English/LTR defaults those pages still render Jalali/Persian dates, and the Jalali dependency cannot actually be removed until these call sites use `formatDate`/`formatDateTime`.

- [P2] Update smoke tests for new locale defaults — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/app/layout.tsx:37-37
  When `siteConfig` falls back to the new English/LTR defaults, `tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts` still asserts `dir="rtl"`, `lang="fa"`, a B Yekan/Vazir font, and Persian header text. This makes `npm run test:e2e` fail immediately after this layout change unless the test assertions or test env are updated with the new default locale/font.
The patch introduces the locale/currency defaults but leaves key currency/date consumers and E2E assertions on the old Persian/Toman/Jalali assumptions. Those inconsistencies would surface in the UI and test suite.

Full review comments:

- [P2] Migrate cart formatter before changing shared currency — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/utils/format.ts:3-7
  With the shared formatter now defaulting to `siteLocale.currency` (USD by default), cart UI still imports `formatPrice` from `src/store/cart-store.ts`, whose local formatter remains hard-coded to `fa-IR` plus `تومان`. Product/search/wishlist surfaces that use this helper will show USD while cart drawer/summary shows Toman for the same prices, so users see inconsistent currencies until the store formatter is removed or wired to the same config.

Under the new English/LTR defaults those pages still render Jalali/Persian dates, and the Jalali dependency cannot actually be removed until these call sites use `formatDate`/`formatDateTime`.

This makes `npm run test:e2e` fail immediately after this layout change unless the test assertions or test env are updated with the new default locale/font.
